                    [32m'requires:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  - start-core\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'sources:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  - TanStack/router:docs/start/framework/react/guide/server-functions.md\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'---\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Server Functions\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Server functions are type-safe RPCs created with `createServerFn`. They run exclusively on the server but can be called from anywhere — loaders, components, hooks, event handlers, or other server functions.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: Server functions are API endpoints. They are reachable independently of whichever route renders the calling UI. **Auth must be enforced inside the handler (or via middleware) for any server function that touches private data.** Route `beforeLoad` is UX, not the data boundary. See [start-core/auth-server-primitives](../auth-server-primitives/SKILL.md) for the session/middleware pattern.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: Loaders are ISOMORPHIC — they run on BOTH client and server. Database queries, file system access, and secret API keys MUST go inside `createServerFn`, NOT in loaders directly.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: Do not use `"use server"` directives, `getServerSideProps`, or any Next.js/Remix server patterns. TanStack Start uses `createServerFn` exclusively.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Basic Usage\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// GET (default)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const getData = createServerFn().handler(async () => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"  return { message: 'Hello from server!' }\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// POST\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const saveData = createServerFn({ method: 'POST' }).handler(async () => {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  return { success: true }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Calling from Loaders\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createFileRoute } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const getPosts = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' }).handler(async () => {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"  const posts = await db.query('SELECT * FROM posts')\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  return { posts }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/posts')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  loader: () => getPosts(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: PostList,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function PostList() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const { posts } = Route.useLoaderData()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <ul>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      {posts.map((p) => (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <li key={p.id}>{p.title}</li>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      ))}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </ul>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Calling from Components\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Use the `useServerFn` hook to call server functions from event handlers:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { useServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const deletePost = createServerFn({ method: 'POST' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  .validator((data: { id: string }) => data)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ data }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    await db.delete('posts').where({ id: data.id })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'    return { success: true }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function DeleteButton({ postId }: { postId: string }) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const deletePostFn = useServerFn(deletePost)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <button onClick={() => deletePostFn({ data: { id: postId } })}>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      Delete\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </button>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Input Validation\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Basic Validator\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const greetUser = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  .validator((data: { name: string }) => data)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ data }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return `Hello, ${data.name}!`\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"await greetUser({ data: { name: 'John' } })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Zod Validator\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { z } from 'zod'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const createUser = createServerFn({ method: 'POST' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  .validator(\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    z.object({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      name: z.string().min(1),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      age: z.number().min(0),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ data }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return `Created user: ${data.name}, age ${data.age}`\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### FormData\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const submitForm = createServerFn({ method: 'POST' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  .validator((data) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (!(data instanceof FormData)) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"      throw new Error('Expected FormData')\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'    }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"      name: data.get('name')?.toString() || '',\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"      email: data.get('email')?.toString() || '',\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'    }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ data }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return { success: true }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Error Handling\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Errors\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const riskyFunction = createServerFn().handler(async () => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"  throw new Error('Something went wrong!')\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'try {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  await riskyFunction()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'} catch (error) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  console.log(error.message) // "Something went wrong!"\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Redirects\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { redirect } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const requireAuth = createServerFn().handler(async () => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const user = await getCurrentUser()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  if (!user) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    throw redirect({ to: '/login' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return user\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Not Found\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { notFound } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const getPost = createServerFn()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .validator((data: { id: string }) => data)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ data }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    const post = await db.findPost(data.id)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    if (!post) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      throw notFound()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return post\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Server Context Utilities\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Access request/response details inside server function handlers:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'import {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  getRequest,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  getRequestHeader,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  setResponseHeaders,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  setResponseStatus,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"} from '@tanstack/react-start/server'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// Public, non-personalized data — safe to cache shared across users.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const getPublicData = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' }).handler(async () => {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  setResponseHeaders({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    // 'public' is correct ONLY when the response does not depend on identity.\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"    // For anything tied to a session/user/tenant, use 'private' or 'no-store'.\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"    'Cache-Control': 'public, max-age=300',\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  setResponseStatus(200)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return fetchPublicData()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"// Authenticated data — must NOT be 'public'.\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"const getMyData = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' }).handler(async () => {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"  const authHeader = getRequestHeader('Authorization')\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  // ... auth check ...\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  setResponseHeaders({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    // 'private' = only the user-agent may cache. Vary by Cookie/Authorization\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'    // so any intermediary that does cache keys by identity, not URL alone.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    'Cache-Control': 'private, max-age=60',\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"    Vary: 'Cookie, Authorization',\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return fetchPersonalizedData()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Available utilities:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `getRequest()` — full Request object\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `getRequestHeader(name)` — single request header\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `setResponseHeader(name, value)` — single response header\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `setResponseHeaders(headers)` — multiple response headers\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `setResponseStatus(code)` — HTTP status code\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## File Organization\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```text\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'src/utils/\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'├── users.functions.ts   # createServerFn wrappers (safe to import anywhere)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'├── users.server.ts      # Server-only helpers (DB queries, internal logic)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'└── schemas.ts           # Shared validation schemas (client-safe)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// users.server.ts — server-only helpers\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { db } from '~/db'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export async function findUserById(id: string) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return db.query.users.findFirst({ where: eq(users.id, id) })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// users.functions.ts — server functions\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { findUserById } from './users.server'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const getUser = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  .validator((data: { id: string }) => data)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ data }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return findUserById(data.id)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Static imports of server functions are safe — the build replaces implementations with RPC stubs in client bundles.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Common Mistakes\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 1. CRITICAL: Relying on a route guard to protect a server function\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"A `beforeLoad` redirect protects the **route's UI**, not the **data endpoint**. `createServerFn` exposes a callable endpoint that an attacker can hit directly — no need to load the route at all. Auth on the endpoint is the security boundary; auth on the route is UX.\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"// WRONG — the route guard doesn't reach the handler\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"const getMyOrders = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' }).handler(async () => {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  return db.orders.findMany() // ← anyone can call the RPC\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/_authenticated/orders')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  beforeLoad: ({ context }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    if (!context.auth.isAuthenticated) throw redirect({ to: '/login' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  },\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  loader: () => getMyOrders(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT — auth enforced on the handler itself\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const getMyOrders = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  .middleware([authMiddleware])\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ context }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return db.orders.findMany({ where: { userId: context.session.userId } })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Apply `authMiddleware` (or an equivalent in-handler check) to **every** `createServerFn` that needs auth. See [start-core/auth-server-primitives](../auth-server-primitives/SKILL.md) for the full session/middleware pattern and [start-core/middleware](../middleware/SKILL.md) for composing the factory.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 2. CRITICAL: Putting server-only code in loaders\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// WRONG — loader is ISOMORPHIC, runs on BOTH client and server\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m''[39m,
                  isTruncated: [33mfalse[39m
                }
              },
              providerOptions: {
                anthropic: {
                  caller: {
                    type: [32m'direct'[39m
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          ]
        },
        {
          role: [32m'assistant'[39m,
          content: [
            {
              type: [32m'text'[39m,
              text: [32m'Now I have a thorough understanding of how TanStack Start works. Let me read the deployment SKILL to understand the server entry points needed:'[39m
            },
            {
              type: [32m'tool-call'[39m,
              toolCallId: [32m'toolu_01Xr3Y66yUzMSmAYGrTEhKKL'[39m,
              toolName: [32m'executeCommand'[39m,
              input: {
                command: [32m'cat /home/user/myproject/node_modules/@tanstack/start-client-core/skills/start-core/deployment/SKILL.md | head -200'[39m
              },
              providerOptions: {
                anthropic: {
                  caller: {
                    type: [32m'direct'[39m
                  }
                }
              }
            }
          ]
        },
        {
          role: [32m'tool'[39m,
          content: [
            {
              type: [32m'tool-result'[39m,
              toolCallId: [32m'toolu_01Xr3Y66yUzMSmAYGrTEhKKL'[39m,
              toolName: [32m'executeCommand'[39m,
              output: {
                type: [32m'json'[39m,
                value: {
                  output: [32m'---\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'name: start-core/deployment\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'description: >-\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Deploy to Cloudflare Workers, Netlify, Vercel, Node.js/Docker,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Bun, Railway. Selective SSR (ssr option per route), SPA mode,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  static prerendering, ISR with Cache-Control headers, SEO and\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  head management.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'type: sub-skill\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'library: tanstack-start\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"library_version: '1.166.2'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'requires:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  - start-core\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'sources:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  - TanStack/router:docs/start/framework/react/guide/hosting.md\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  - TanStack/router:docs/start/framework/react/guide/selective-ssr.md\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  - TanStack/router:docs/start/framework/react/guide/static-prerendering.md\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  - TanStack/router:docs/start/framework/react/guide/seo.md\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'---\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# Deployment and Rendering\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'TanStack Start deploys to any hosting provider via Vite and Nitro. This skill covers hosting setup, SSR configuration, prerendering, and SEO.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Hosting Providers\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Cloudflare Workers\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'pnpm add -D @cloudflare/vite-plugin wrangler\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// vite.config.ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { defineConfig } from 'vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { tanstackStart } from '@tanstack/react-start/plugin/vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { cloudflare } from '@cloudflare/vite-plugin'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import viteReact from '@vitejs/plugin-react'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export default defineConfig({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  plugins: [\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    cloudflare({ viteEnvironment: { name: 'ssr' } }),\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'    tanstackStart(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    viteReact(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  ],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```jsonc\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// wrangler.jsonc\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'{\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "name": "my-app",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "compatibility_date": "2025-09-02",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "compatibility_flags": ["nodejs_compat"],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "main": "@tanstack/react-start/server-entry",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Deploy: `npx wrangler login && pnpm run deploy`\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **Worker env is per-request.** Cloudflare Workers inject env vars at request time. `process.env.X` at module scope evaluates to `undefined` even on the server. The Cloudflare-canonical way to read env (including from module scope) is the `cloudflare:workers` env binding:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> ```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"> import { env } from 'cloudflare:workers'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'> const apiHost = env.API_HOST\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> ```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"> Or read `process.env.X` per-request inside `.handler()` / middleware `.server()`. See [Cloudflare's environment-variables docs](https://developers.cloudflare.com/workers/configuration/environment-variables/) and [start-core/execution-model](../execution-model/SKILL.md).\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Netlify\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'pnpm add -D @netlify/vite-plugin-tanstack-start\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// vite.config.ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { defineConfig } from 'vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { tanstackStart } from '@tanstack/react-start/plugin/vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import netlify from '@netlify/vite-plugin-tanstack-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import viteReact from '@vitejs/plugin-react'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export default defineConfig({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  plugins: [tanstackStart(), netlify(), viteReact()],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Deploy: `npx netlify deploy`\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Nitro (Vercel, Railway, Node.js, Docker)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'npm install nitro@npm:nitro-nightly@latest\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// vite.config.ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { defineConfig } from 'vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { tanstackStart } from '@tanstack/react-start/plugin/vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { nitro } from 'nitro/vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import viteReact from '@vitejs/plugin-react'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export default defineConfig({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  plugins: [tanstackStart(), nitro(), viteReact()],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Build and start: `npm run build && node .output/server/index.mjs`\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Bun\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Bun deployment requires React 19. For React 18, use Node.js deployment.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// vite.config.ts — add bun preset to nitro\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"plugins: [tanstackStart(), nitro({ preset: 'bun' }), viteReact()]\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Selective SSR\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Control SSR per route with the `ssr` property.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### `ssr: true` (default)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Runs `beforeLoad` and `loader` on server, renders component on server:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/posts/$postId')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  ssr: true, // default\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  loader: () => fetchPost(), // runs on server during SSR\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: PostPage, // rendered on server\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### `ssr: false`\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Disables server execution of `beforeLoad`/`loader` and server rendering:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/dashboard')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  ssr: false,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  loader: () => fetchDashboard(), // runs on client only\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: DashboardPage, // rendered on client only\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"### `ssr: 'data-only'`\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Runs `beforeLoad`/`loader` on server but renders component on client only:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/canvas')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"  ssr: 'data-only',\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  loader: () => fetchCanvasData(), // runs on server\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: CanvasPage, // rendered on client only\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Functional Form\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Decide SSR at runtime based on params/search:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/docs/$docType/$docId')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  ssr: ({ params }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"    if (params.status === 'success' && params.value.docType === 'sheet') {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'      return false\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  },\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### SSR Inheritance\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Children inherit parent SSR config and can only be MORE restrictive:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `true` → `data-only` or `false` (allowed)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `false` → `true` (NOT allowed — parent `false` wins)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### Default SSR\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Change the default for all routes in `src/start.ts`:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createStart } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export const startInstance = createStart(() => ({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  defaultSsr: false,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}))\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Static Prerendering\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'    enabled: true,\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### `ssr: false`\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'{ "compatibility_flags": ["nodejs_compat"] }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 2. MEDIUM: Bun deployment with React 18\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 3. MEDIUM: Child route loosening parent SSR config\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'  ssr: true, // IGNORED — parent false wins\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT — children can only be MORE restrictive\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'  ssr: false, // OK — more restrictive than parent\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +

            [32m'Git Safety Protocol:\n'[39m +
            [32m'- NEVER update the git config\n'[39m +
            [32m"- NEVER run destructive git commands (push --force, reset --hard, checkout ., restore ., clean -f, branch -D) unless the user explicitly requests these actions.             [32m'- NEVER skip hooks (--no-verify, --no-gpg-sign, etc) unless the user explicitly requests it\n'[39m +

            [32m'- CRITICAL: Always create NEW commits rather than amending, unless the user explicitly requests a git amend. Instead, after hook failure, fix the issue, re-stage, and create a NEW commit\n'[39m +
            [32m'- When staging files, prefer adding specific files by name rather than using "git add -A" or "git add .", which can accidentally include sensitive files (.env, credentials) or large binaries\n'[39m +

                    [32m'# React Start (`@tanstack/react-start`)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'This skill builds on start-core. Read [start-core](../../../start-client-core/skills/start-core/SKILL.md) first for foundational concepts.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'This skill covers the React-specific bindings, setup, and patterns for TanStack Start.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'For React Server Components patterns, see [react-start/server-components](./server-components/SKILL.md).\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: All code is ISOMORPHIC by default. Loaders run on BOTH server and client. Use `createServerFn` for server-only logic.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: Do not confuse `@tanstack/react-start` with Next.js or Remix. They are completely different frameworks with different APIs.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: Types are FULLY INFERRED. Never cast, never annotate inferred values.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Package API Surface\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`@tanstack/react-start` re-exports everything from `@tanstack/start-client-core` plus:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useServerFn` — React hook for calling server functions from components\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'All core APIs (`createServerFn`, `createMiddleware`, `createStart`, `createIsomorphicFn`, `createServerOnlyFn`, `createClientOnlyFn`) are available from `@tanstack/react-start`.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Server utilities (`getRequest`, `getRequestHeader`, `setResponseHeader`, `setResponseHeaders`, `setResponseStatus`) are imported from `@tanstack/react-start/server`.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Full Project Setup\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 1. Install Dependencies\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'npm i @tanstack/react-start @tanstack/react-router react react-dom\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'npm i -D vite @vitejs/plugin-react typescript @types/react @types/react-dom\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 2. package.json\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```json\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'{\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "type": "module",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "scripts": {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "dev": "vite dev",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "build": "vite build",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "start": "node .output/server/index.mjs"\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 3. tsconfig.json\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```json\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'{\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  "compilerOptions": {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "jsx": "react-jsx",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "moduleResolution": "Bundler",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "module": "ESNext",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "target": "ES2022",\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "skipLibCheck": true,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    "strictNullChecks": true\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 4. vite.config.ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { defineConfig } from 'vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { tanstackStart } from '@tanstack/react-start/plugin/vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import viteReact from '@vitejs/plugin-react'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export default defineConfig({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  plugins: [\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    tanstackStart(), // MUST come before react()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    viteReact(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  ],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 5. Router Factory (src/router.tsx)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createRouter } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { routeTree } from './routeTree.gen'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export function getRouter() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const router = createRouter({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    routeTree,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    scrollRestoration: true,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return router\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 6. Root Route (src/routes/\\_\\_root.tsx)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import type { ReactNode } from 'react'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'import {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Outlet,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  createRootRoute,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  HeadContent,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Scripts,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"} from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export const Route = createRootRoute({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  head: () => ({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    meta: [\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"      { charSet: 'utf-8' },\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"      { name: 'viewport', content: 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1' },\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"      { title: 'My TanStack Start App' },\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'    ],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: RootComponent,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function RootComponent() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <RootDocument>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <Outlet />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </RootDocument>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function RootDocument({ children }: Readonly<{ children: ReactNode }>) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <HeadContent />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        {children}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <Scripts />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 7. Index Route (src/routes/index.tsx)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createFileRoute } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const getGreeting = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' }).handler(async () => {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"  return 'Hello from TanStack Start!'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  loader: () => getGreeting(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: HomePage,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function HomePage() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const greeting = Route.useLoaderData()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return <h1>{greeting}</h1>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## useServerFn Hook\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Use `useServerFn` to call server functions from React components with proper integration:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn, useServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const updatePost = createServerFn({ method: 'POST' })\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  .validator((data: { id: string; title: string }) => data)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  .handler(async ({ data }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    await db.posts.update(data.id, { title: data.title })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    return { success: true }\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function EditPostForm({ postId }: { postId: string }) {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const updatePostFn = useServerFn(updatePost)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"  const [title, setTitle] = useState('')\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <form\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      onSubmit={async (e) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        e.preventDefault()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        await updatePostFn({ data: { id: postId, title } })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      }}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    >\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <input value={title} onChange={(e) => setTitle(e.target.value)} />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <button type="submit">Save</button>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </form>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Global Start Configuration (src/start.ts)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createStart, createMiddleware } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const requestLogger = createMiddleware().server(async ({ next, request }) => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  console.log(`${request.method} ${request.url}`)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return next()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export const startInstance = createStart(() => ({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  requestMiddleware: [requestLogger],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}))\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## React-Specific Components\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'All routing components from `@tanstack/react-router` work in Start:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<RouterProvider>` — not needed in Start (handled automatically)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<Outlet>` — renders matched child route\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<Link>` — type-safe navigation\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<Navigate>` — declarative redirect\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<HeadContent>` — renders head tags (must be in `<head>`)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<Scripts>` — renders body scripts (must be in `<body>`)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<Await>` — renders deferred data with Suspense\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<ClientOnly>` — renders children only after hydration\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `<CatchBoundary>` — error boundary\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Hooks Reference\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'All hooks from `@tanstack/react-router` work in Start:\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useRouter()` — router instance\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useRouterState()` — subscribe to router state\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useNavigate()` — programmatic navigation\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useSearch({ from })` — validated search params\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useParams({ from })` — path params\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useLoaderData({ from })` — loader data\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useMatch({ from })` — full route match\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `useRouteContext({ from })` — route context\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `Route.useLoaderData()` — typed loader data (preferred in route files)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'- `Route.useSearch()` — typed search params (preferred in route files)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Common Mistakes\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 1. CRITICAL: Importing from wrong package\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// WRONG — this is the SPA router, NOT Start\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT — server functions come from react-start\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT — routing APIs come from react-router (re-exported by Start too)\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createFileRoute, Link } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 2. HIGH: Using React hooks in beforeLoad or loader\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// WRONG — beforeLoad/loader are NOT React components\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'beforeLoad: () => {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const auth = useAuth() // React hook, cannot be used here\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT — pass state via router context\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'const rootRoute = createRootRouteWithContext<{ auth: AuthState }>()({})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 3. HIGH: Missing Scripts component\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"Without `<Scripts />` in the root route's `<body>`, client JavaScript doesn't load and the app won't hydrate.\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Cross-References\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'- [react-router](../../../react-router/skills/react-router/SKILL.md) — React Router hooks and components\r\n'[39m +

                  isTruncated: [33mfalse[39m

              toolName: [32m'executeCommand'[39m,
              output: {
                type: [32m'json'[39m,
                value: {
                  output: [32m'---\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'description: >-\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Core overview for TanStack Start: tanstackStart() Vite plugin,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  getRouter() factory, root route document shell (HeadContent,\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'---\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'# TanStack Start Core\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'TanStack Start is a full-stack React framework built on TanStack Router and Vite. It adds SSR, streaming, server functions (type-safe RPCs), middleware, server routes, and universal deployment.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: All code in TanStack Start is ISOMORPHIC by default — it runs in BOTH server and client environments. Loaders run on both server AND client. To run code exclusively on the server, use `createServerFn`. This is the #1 AI agent mistake.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: TanStack Start is NOT Next.js. Do not generate `getServerSideProps`, `"use server"` directives, `app/layout.tsx`, or any Next.js/Remix patterns. Use `createServerFn` for server-only code.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'> **CRITICAL**: Types are FULLY INFERRED. Never cast, never annotate inferred values.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Sub-Skills\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Task                                             | Sub-Skill                                                                       |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| ------------------------------------------------ | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Type-safe RPCs, data fetching, mutations         | [start-core/server-functions/SKILL.md](./server-functions/SKILL.md)             |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Request/function middleware, context, auth       | [start-core/middleware/SKILL.md](./middleware/SKILL.md)                         |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Server-side auth: sessions, cookies, OAuth, CSRF | [start-core/auth-server-primitives/SKILL.md](./auth-server-primitives/SKILL.md) |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Isomorphic execution, environment boundaries     | [start-core/execution-model/SKILL.md](./execution-model/SKILL.md)               |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| REST API endpoints alongside app routes          | [start-core/server-routes/SKILL.md](./server-routes/SKILL.md)                   |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'| Hosting, SSR modes, prerendering, SEO            | [start-core/deployment/SKILL.md](./deployment/SKILL.md)                         |\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Quick Decision Tree\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```text\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Need to run code exclusively on the server (DB, secrets)?\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  → start-core/server-functions\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Need auth checks, logging, or shared logic across server functions?\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  → start-core/middleware\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Need to add login, sessions, OAuth, CSRF, password reset?\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  → start-core/auth-server-primitives\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Need to understand where code runs (server vs client)?\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  → start-core/execution-model\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Need a REST API endpoint (GET/POST/PUT/DELETE)?\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  → start-core/server-routes\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'Need to deploy, configure SSR, or prerender?\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  → start-core/deployment\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Project Setup\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 1. Install Dependencies\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```bash\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'npm i @tanstack/react-start @tanstack/react-router react react-dom\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'npm i -D vite @vitejs/plugin-react typescript\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 2. Configure Vite\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// vite.config.ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { defineConfig } from 'vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { tanstackStart } from '@tanstack/react-start/plugin/vite'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import viteReact from '@vitejs/plugin-react'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export default defineConfig({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  plugins: [\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    // MUST come before react()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    tanstackStart(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    viteReact(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  ],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 3. Create Router Factory\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// src/router.tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createRouter } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { routeTree } from './routeTree.gen'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export function getRouter() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const router = createRouter({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    routeTree,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    scrollRestoration: true,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  })\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return router\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 4. Create Root Route with Document Shell\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// src/routes/__root.tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import type { ReactNode } from 'react'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'import {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Outlet,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  createRootRoute,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  HeadContent,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Scripts,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"} from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'export const Route = createRootRoute({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  head: () => ({\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    meta: [\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"      { charSet: 'utf-8' },\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"      { name: 'viewport', content: 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1' },\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"      { title: 'My App' },\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'    ],\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  }),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: RootComponent,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function RootComponent() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <HeadContent />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <Outlet />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <Scripts />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 5. Create Index Route with Server Function\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// src/routes/index.tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"import { createFileRoute } from '@tanstack/react-router'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"import { createServerFn } from '@tanstack/react-start'\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"const getGreeting = createServerFn({ method: 'GET' }).handler(async () => {\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m"  return { message: 'Hello from the server!' }\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m"export const Route = createFileRoute('/')({\r\n"[39m +
                    [32m'  loader: () => getGreeting(),\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  component: HomePage,\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'})\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function HomePage() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  const data = Route.useLoaderData()\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return <h1>{data.message}</h1>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Common Mistakes\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 1. CRITICAL: React plugin before Start plugin in Vite config\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```ts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// WRONG — route generation and server function compilation fail\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'plugins: [react(), tanstackStart()]\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT — Start plugin must come first\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'plugins: [tanstackStart(), react()]\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 2. HIGH: Enabling verbatimModuleSyntax in tsconfig\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'`verbatimModuleSyntax` causes server bundles to leak into client bundles. Keep it disabled.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'### 3. HIGH: Missing Scripts component in root route\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'The `<Scripts />` component must be rendered in the `<body>` of the root route. Without it, client-side JavaScript does not load and hydration fails.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```tsx\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// WRONG — no Scripts\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function RootComponent() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <HeadContent />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <Outlet />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'// CORRECT — Scripts in body\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'function RootComponent() {\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  return (\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    <html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <HeadContent />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </head>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      <body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <Outlet />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'        <Scripts />\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'      </body>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'    </html>\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  )\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'}\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'```\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'## Version Note\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'This skill targets `@tanstack/react-start` v1.166.2 and `@tanstack/start-client-core` v1.166.2.\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m''[39m,
                  isTruncated: [33mfalse[39m
                }
              },
              providerOptions: {

                }

          ]

            }
          ]
        },
        {
          role: [32m'tool'[39m,
          content: [
            {
              type: [32m'tool-result'[39m,
              toolCallId: [32m'toolu_014ZudnWZb5naX1dKufsKN8f'[39m,
              toolName: [32m'executeCommand'[39m,
              output: {
                type: [32m'json'[39m,
                value: {
                  output: [32m'---\r\n'[39m +

                    [32m'description: >-\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  Server-side API endpoints using the server property on\r\n'[39m +
                    [32m'  createFileRoute, HTTP method handlers (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE),\r\n'[39m +
